39 object Applications {
40   import tpd._
41 
42   def extractorMember(tp: Type, name: Name)(implicit ctx: Context) =
43     tp.member(name).suchThat(_.info.isParameterless)
44 
45   def extractorMemberType(tp: Type, name: Name, errorPos: Position = NoPosition)(implicit ctx: Context) = {
46     val ref = extractorMember(tp, name)
47     if (ref.isOverloaded)
48       errorType(i"Overloaded reference to $ref is not allowed in extractor", errorPos)
49     ref.info.widenExpr.annotatedToRepeated.dealias
50   }
51 
52   /** Does `tp` fit the "product match" conditions as an unapply result type
53    *  for a pattern with `numArgs` subpatterns?
54    *  This is the case of `tp` has members `_1` to `_N` where `N == numArgs`.
55    */
56   def isProductMatch(tp: Type, numArgs: Int)(implicit ctx: Context) =
57     numArgs > 0 && productArity(tp) == numArgs
58 
59   /** Does `tp` fit the "get match" conditions as an unapply result type?
60    *  This is the case of `tp` has a `get` member as well as a
61    *  parameterless `isDefined` member of result type `Boolean`.
62    */
63   def isGetMatch(tp: Type, errorPos: Position = NoPosition)(implicit ctx: Context) =
64     extractorMemberType(tp, nme.isEmpty, errorPos).isRef(defn.BooleanClass) &&
65     extractorMemberType(tp, nme.get, errorPos).exists
66 
67   def productSelectorTypes(tp: Type, errorPos: Position = NoPosition)(implicit ctx: Context): List[Type] = {
68     val sels = for (n <- Iterator.from(0)) yield extractorMemberType(tp, nme.selectorName(n), errorPos)
69     sels.takeWhile(_.exists).toList
70   }
71 
72   def productArity(tp: Type)(implicit ctx: Context) =
73     if (defn.isProductSubType(tp)) productSelectorTypes(tp).size else -1
74 
75   def productSelectors(tp: Type)(implicit ctx: Context): List[Symbol] = {
76     val sels = for (n <- Iterator.from(0)) yield
77       tp.member(nme.selectorName(n)).suchThat(_.info.isParameterless).symbol
78     sels.takeWhile(_.exists).toList
79   }
80 
81   def getUnapplySelectors(tp: Type, args: List[untpd.Tree], pos: Position = NoPosition)(implicit ctx: Context): List[Type] =
82     if (args.length > 1 && !(tp.derivesFrom(defn.SeqClass))) {
83       val sels = productSelectorTypes(tp, pos)
84       if (sels.length == args.length) sels
85       else tp :: Nil
86     } else tp :: Nil
87 
88   def unapplyArgs(unapplyResult: Type, unapplyFn: Tree, args: List[untpd.Tree], pos: Position = NoPosition)(implicit ctx: Context): List[Type] = {
89 
90     val unapplyName = unapplyFn.symbol.name
91     def seqSelector = defn.RepeatedParamType.appliedTo(unapplyResult.elemType :: Nil)
92     def getTp = extractorMemberType(unapplyResult, nme.get, pos)
93 
94     def fail = {
95       val addendum =
96         if (ctx.scala2Mode && unapplyName == nme.unapplySeq)
97           "\nYou might want to try to rewrite the extractor to use `unapply` instead."
98       ctx.error(em"$unapplyResult is not a valid result type of an $unapplyName method of an extractor$addendum", pos)
99       Nil
100     }
101 
102     if (unapplyName == nme.unapplySeq) {
103       if (unapplyResult derivesFrom defn.SeqClass) seqSelector :: Nil
104       else if (isGetMatch(unapplyResult, pos)) {
105         val seqArg = getTp.elemType.hiBound
106         if (seqArg.exists) args.map(Function.const(seqArg))
107         else fail
108       }
109       else fail
110     }
111     else {
112       assert(unapplyName == nme.unapply)
113       if (isProductMatch(unapplyResult, args.length))
114         productSelectorTypes(unapplyResult)
115       else if (isGetMatch(unapplyResult, pos))
116         getUnapplySelectors(getTp, args, pos)
117       else if (unapplyResult isRef defn.BooleanClass)
118         Nil
119       else if (defn.isProductSubType(unapplyResult))
120         productSelectorTypes(unapplyResult)
121           // this will cause a "wrong number of arguments in pattern" error later on,
122           // which is better than the message in `fail`.
123       else fail
124     }
125   }
126 
127   def wrapDefs(defs: mutable.ListBuffer[Tree], tree: Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree =
128     if (defs != null && defs.nonEmpty) tpd.Block(defs.toList, tree) else tree
129 }

140   /** @tparam Arg       the type of arguments, could be tpd.Tree, untpd.Tree, or Type
141    *  @param methRef    the reference to the method of the application
142    *  @param funType    the type of the function part of the application
143    *  @param args       the arguments of the application
144    *  @param resultType the expected result type of the application
145    */
146   abstract class Application[Arg](methRef: TermRef, funType: Type, args: List[Arg], resultType: Type)(implicit ctx: Context) {
147 
148     /** The type of typed arguments: either tpd.Tree or Type */
149     type TypedArg
150 
151     /** Given an original argument and the type of the corresponding formal
152      *  parameter, produce a typed argument.
153      */
154     protected def typedArg(arg: Arg, formal: Type): TypedArg
155 
156     /** Turn a typed tree into an argument */
157     protected def treeToArg(arg: Tree): Arg
158 
159     /** Check that argument corresponds to type `formal` and
160      *  possibly add it to the list of adapted arguments
161      */
162     protected def addArg(arg: TypedArg, formal: Type): Unit
163 
164     /** Is this an argument of the form `expr: _*` or a RepeatedParamType
165      *  derived from such an argument?
166      */
167     protected def isVarArg(arg: Arg): Boolean
168 
169     /** If constructing trees, turn last `n` processed arguments into a
170      *  `SeqLiteral` tree with element type `elemFormal`.
171      */
172     protected def makeVarArg(n: Int, elemFormal: Type): Unit
173 
174     /** If all `args` have primitive numeric types, make sure it's the same one */
175     protected def harmonizeArgs(args: List[TypedArg]): List[TypedArg]
176 
177     /** Signal failure with given message at position of given argument */
178     protected def fail(msg: => Message, arg: Arg): Unit
179 
180     /** Signal failure with given message at position of the application itself */
181     protected def fail(msg: => Message): Unit
182 
183     protected def appPos: Position
184 
185     /** The current function part, which might be affected by lifting.
186      */
187     protected def normalizedFun: Tree
188 
189     protected def typeOfArg(arg: Arg): Type
190 
191     /** If constructing trees, pull out all parts of the function
192      *  which are not idempotent into separate prefix definitions
193      */
194     protected def liftFun(): Unit = ()
195 
196     /** A flag signalling that the typechecking the application was so far successful */
197     private[this] var _ok = true
198 
199     def ok = _ok
200     def ok_=(x: Boolean) = {
201       assert(x || ctx.reporter.errorsReported || !ctx.typerState.isCommittable) // !!! DEBUG
202       _ok = x
203     }
204 
205     /** The function's type after widening and instantiating polytypes
206      *  with TypeParamRefs in constraint set
207      */
208     val methType = funType.widen match {
209       case funType: MethodType => funType
210       case funType: PolyType => constrained(funType).resultType
211       case tp => tp //was: funType
212     }
213 
214     /** The arguments re-ordered so that each named argument matches the
215      *  same-named formal parameter.
216      */
217     lazy val orderedArgs =
218       if (hasNamedArg(args))
219         reorder(args.asInstanceOf[List[untpd.Tree]]).asInstanceOf[List[Arg]]
220       else
221         args
222 
223     protected def init() = methType match {
224       case methType: MethodType =>
225         // apply the result type constraint, unless method type is dependent
226         val resultApprox = resultTypeApprox(methType)
227         if (!constrainResult(resultApprox, resultType))
228           if (ctx.typerState.isCommittable)
229             // defer the problem until after the application;
230             // it might be healed by an implicit conversion
231             ()
232           else
233             fail(err.typeMismatchMsg(methType.resultType, resultType))
234         // match all arguments with corresponding formal parameters
235         matchArgs(orderedArgs, methType.paramInfos, 0)
236       case _ =>
237         if (methType.isError) ok = false
238         else fail(s"$methString does not take parameters")
239     }
240 
241     /** The application was successful */
242     def success = ok
243 
244     protected def methodType = methType.asInstanceOf[MethodType]
245     private def methString: String = i"${methRef.symbol}: ${methType.show}"
246 
247     /** Re-order arguments to correctly align named arguments */
248     def reorder[T >: Untyped](args: List[Trees.Tree[T]]): List[Trees.Tree[T]] = {
249 
250       /** @param pnames    The list of parameter names that are missing arguments
251        *  @param args      The list of arguments that are not yet passed, or that are waiting to be dropped
252        *  @param nameToArg A map from as yet unseen names to named arguments
253        *  @param toDrop    A set of names that have already be passed as named arguments
254        *
255        *  For a well-typed application we have the invariants
256        *
257        *  1. `(args diff toDrop)` can be reordered to match `pnames`
258        *  2. For every `(name -> arg)` in `nameToArg`, `arg` is an element of `args`
259        */
260       def handleNamed(pnames: List[Name], args: List[Trees.Tree[T]],
261                       nameToArg: Map[Name, Trees.NamedArg[T]], toDrop: Set[Name]): List[Trees.Tree[T]] = pnames match {
262         case pname :: pnames1 if nameToArg contains pname =>
263           // there is a named argument for this parameter; pick it
264           nameToArg(pname) :: handleNamed(pnames1, args, nameToArg - pname, toDrop + pname)
265         case _ =>
266           def pnamesRest = if (pnames.isEmpty) pnames else pnames.tail
267           args match {
268             case (arg @ NamedArg(aname, _)) :: args1 =>
269               if (toDrop contains aname) // argument is already passed
270                 handleNamed(pnames, args1, nameToArg, toDrop - aname)
271               else if ((nameToArg contains aname) && pnames.nonEmpty) // argument is missing, pass an empty tree
272                 genericEmptyTree :: handleNamed(pnames.tail, args, nameToArg, toDrop)
273               else { // name not (or no longer) available for named arg
274                 def msg =
275                   if (methodType.paramNames contains aname)
276                     s"parameter $aname of $methString is already instantiated"
277                   else
278                     s"$methString does not have a parameter $aname"
279                 fail(msg, arg.asInstanceOf[Arg])
280                 arg :: handleNamed(pnamesRest, args1, nameToArg, toDrop)
281               }
282             case arg :: args1 =>
283               arg :: handleNamed(pnamesRest, args1, nameToArg, toDrop) // unnamed argument; pick it
284             case Nil => // no more args, continue to pick up any preceding named args
285               if (pnames.isEmpty) Nil
286               else handleNamed(pnamesRest, args, nameToArg, toDrop)
287           }
288       }
289 
290       def handlePositional(pnames: List[Name], args: List[Trees.Tree[T]]): List[Trees.Tree[T]] =
291         args match {
292           case (arg: NamedArg @unchecked) :: _ =>
293             val nameAssocs = for (arg @ NamedArg(name, _) <- args) yield (name, arg)
294             handleNamed(pnames, args, nameAssocs.toMap, Set())
295           case arg :: args1 =>
296             arg :: handlePositional(if (pnames.isEmpty) Nil else pnames.tail, args1)
297           case Nil => Nil
298         }
299 
300       handlePositional(methodType.paramNames, args)
301     }
302 
303     /** Splice new method reference into existing application */
304     def spliceMeth(meth: Tree, app: Tree): Tree = app match {
305       case Apply(fn, args) =>
306         spliceMeth(meth, fn).appliedToArgs(args)
307       case TypeApply(fn, targs) =>
308         // Note: It is important that the type arguments `targs` are passed in new trees
309         // instead of being spliced in literally. Otherwise, a type argument to a default
310         // method could be constructed as the definition site of the type variable for
311         // that default constructor. This would interpolate type variables too early,
312         // causing lots of tests (among them tasty_unpickleScala2) to fail.
313         //
314         // The test case is in i1757.scala. Here we have a variable `s` and a method `cpy`
315         // defined like this:
316         //
317         //      var s
318         //      def cpy[X](b: List[Int] = b): B[X] = new B[X](b)
319         //
320         // The call `s.cpy()` then gets expanded to
321         //
322         //      { val $1$: B[Int] = this.s
323         //        $1$.cpy[X']($1$.cpy$default$1[X']
324         //      }
325         //
326         // A type variable gets interpolated if it does not appear in the type
327         // of the current tree and the current tree contains the variable's "definition".
328         // Previously, the polymorphic function tree to which the variable was first added
329         // was taken as the variable's definition. But that fails here because that
330         // tree was `s.cpy` but got transformed into `$1$.cpy`. We now take the type argument
331         // [X'] of the variable as its definition tree, which is more robust. But then
332         // it's crucial that the type tree is not copied directly as argument to
333         // `cpy$default$1`. If it was, the variable `X'` would already be interpolated
334         // when typing the default argument, which is too early.
335         spliceMeth(meth, fn).appliedToTypes(targs.tpes)
336       case _ => meth
337     }
338 
339     /** Find reference to default parameter getter for parameter #n in current
340      *  parameter list, or NoType if none was found
341      */
342     def findDefaultGetter(n: Int)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = {
343       val meth = methRef.symbol.asTerm
344       val receiver: Tree = methPart(normalizedFun) match {
345         case Select(receiver, _) => receiver
346         case mr => mr.tpe.normalizedPrefix match {
347           case mr: TermRef => ref(mr)
348           case mr =>
349             if (this.isInstanceOf[TestApplication[_]])
350               // In this case it is safe to skolemize now; we will produce a stable prefix for the actual call.
351               ref(mr.narrow)
352             else
353               EmptyTree
354         }
355       }
356       val getterPrefix =
357         if ((meth is Synthetic) && meth.name == nme.apply) nme.CONSTRUCTOR else meth.name
358       def getterName = DefaultGetterName(getterPrefix, n)
359       if (!meth.hasDefaultParams)
360         EmptyTree
361       else if (receiver.isEmpty) {
362         def findGetter(cx: Context): Tree = {
363           if (cx eq NoContext) EmptyTree
364           else if (cx.scope != cx.outer.scope &&
365             cx.denotNamed(meth.name).hasAltWith(_.symbol == meth)) {
366             val denot = cx.denotNamed(getterName)
367             if (denot.exists) ref(TermRef(cx.owner.thisType, getterName, denot))
368             else {
369               assert(ctx.mode.is(Mode.Interactive),
370                 s"non-existent getter denotation ($denot) for getter($getterName)")
371               findGetter(cx.outer)
372             }
373           } else findGetter(cx.outer)
374         }
375         findGetter(ctx)
376       }
377       else {
378         def selectGetter(qual: Tree): Tree = {
379           val getterDenot = qual.tpe.member(getterName)
380           if (getterDenot.exists) qual.select(TermRef(qual.tpe, getterName, getterDenot))
381           else EmptyTree
382         }
383         if (!meth.isClassConstructor)
384           selectGetter(receiver)
385         else {
386           // default getters for class constructors are found in the companion object
387           val cls = meth.owner
388           val companion = cls.companionModule
389           if (companion.isTerm) {
390             val prefix = receiver.tpe.baseType(cls).normalizedPrefix
391             if (prefix.exists) selectGetter(ref(TermRef(prefix, companion.asTerm)))
392             else EmptyTree
393           }
394           else EmptyTree
395         }
396       }
397     }
398 
399     /** Is `sym` a constructor of a Java-defined annotation? */
400     def isJavaAnnotConstr(sym: Symbol) =
401       sym.is(JavaDefined) && sym.isConstructor && sym.owner.derivesFrom(defn.AnnotationClass)
402 
403     /** Match re-ordered arguments against formal parameters
404      *  @param n   The position of the first parameter in formals in `methType`.
405      */
406     def matchArgs(args: List[Arg], formals: List[Type], n: Int): Unit = {
407       if (success) formals match {
408         case formal :: formals1 =>
409 
410           /** Add result of typing argument `arg` against parameter type `formal`.
411            *  @return  A type transformation to apply to all arguments following this one.
412            */
413           def addTyped(arg: Arg, formal: Type): Type => Type = {
414             addArg(typedArg(arg, formal), formal)
415             if (methodType.isParamDependent)
416               safeSubstParam(_, methodType.paramRefs(n), typeOfArg(arg))
417             else identity
418           }
419 
420           def missingArg(n: Int): Unit = {
421             val pname = methodType.paramNames(n)
422             fail(
423               if (pname.firstPart contains '$') s"not enough arguments for $methString"
424               else s"missing argument for parameter $pname of $methString")
425           }
426 
427           def tryDefault(n: Int, args1: List[Arg]): Unit = {
428             if (!isJavaAnnotConstr(methRef.symbol))
429               liftFun()
430             val getter = findDefaultGetter(n + numArgs(normalizedFun))
431             if (getter.isEmpty) missingArg(n)
432             else {
433               val substParam = addTyped(
434                   treeToArg(spliceMeth(getter withPos normalizedFun.pos, normalizedFun)),
435                   formal)
436               matchArgs(args1, formals1.mapconserve(substParam), n + 1)
437             }
438           }
439 
440           if (formal.isRepeatedParam)
441             args match {
442               case arg :: Nil if isVarArg(arg) =>
443                 addTyped(arg, formal)
444               case _ =>
445                 val elemFormal = formal.widenExpr.argTypesLo.head
446                 val typedArgs = harmonic(harmonizeArgs)(args.map(typedArg(_, elemFormal)))
447                 typedArgs.foreach(addArg(_, elemFormal))
448                 makeVarArg(args.length, elemFormal)
449             }
450           else args match {
451             case EmptyTree :: args1 =>
452               tryDefault(n, args1)
453             case arg :: args1 =>
454               val substParam = addTyped(arg, formal)
455               matchArgs(args1, formals1.mapconserve(substParam), n + 1)
456             case nil =>
457               tryDefault(n, args)
458           }
459 
460         case nil =>
461           args match {
462             case arg :: args1 => fail(s"too many arguments for $methString", arg)
463             case nil =>
464           }
465       }
466     }
467   }
468 
469   /** Subclass of Application for the cases where we are interested only
470    *  in a "can/cannot apply" answer, without needing to construct trees or
471    *  issue error messages.
472    */
473   abstract class TestApplication[Arg](methRef: TermRef, funType: Type, args: List[Arg], resultType: Type)(implicit ctx: Context)
474   extends Application[Arg](methRef, funType, args, resultType) {
475     type TypedArg = Arg
476     type Result = Unit
477 
478     protected def argOK(arg: TypedArg, formal: Type) = argType(arg, formal) match {
479       case ref: TermRef if ref.denot.isOverloaded =>
480         // in this case we could not resolve overloading because no alternative
481         // matches expected type
482         false
483       case argtpe =>
484         def SAMargOK = formal match {
485           case SAMType(meth) => argtpe <:< meth.info.toFunctionType()
486           case _ => false
487         }
488         isCompatible(argtpe, formal) || ctx.mode.is(Mode.ImplicitsEnabled) && SAMargOK
489     }
490 
491     /** The type of the given argument */
492     protected def argType(arg: Arg, formal: Type): Type
493 
494     def typedArg(arg: Arg, formal: Type): Arg = arg
495     final def addArg(arg: TypedArg, formal: Type) = ok = ok & argOK(arg, formal)
496     def makeVarArg(n: Int, elemFormal: Type) = {}
497     def fail(msg: => Message, arg: Arg) =
498       ok = false
499     def fail(msg: => Message) =
500       ok = false
501     def appPos = NoPosition
502     lazy val normalizedFun = ref(methRef)
503     init()
504   }

506   /** Subclass of Application for applicability tests with type arguments and value
507    *  argument trees.
508    */
509   class ApplicableToTrees(methRef: TermRef, targs: List[Type], args: List[Tree], resultType: Type)(implicit ctx: Context)
510   extends TestApplication(methRef, methRef.widen.appliedTo(targs), args, resultType) {
511     def argType(arg: Tree, formal: Type): Type = normalize(arg.tpe, formal)
512     def treeToArg(arg: Tree): Tree = arg
513     def isVarArg(arg: Tree): Boolean = tpd.isWildcardStarArg(arg)
514     def typeOfArg(arg: Tree): Type = arg.tpe
515     def harmonizeArgs(args: List[Tree]) = harmonize(args)
516   }

518   /** Subclass of Application for applicability tests with type arguments and value
519    * argument trees.
520    */
521   class ApplicableToTreesDirectly(methRef: TermRef, targs: List[Type], args: List[Tree], resultType: Type)(implicit ctx: Context) extends ApplicableToTrees(methRef, targs, args, resultType)(ctx) {
522     override def argOK(arg: TypedArg, formal: Type) = argType(arg, formal) <:< formal
523   }

525   /** Subclass of Application for applicability tests with value argument types. */
526   class ApplicableToTypes(methRef: TermRef, args: List[Type], resultType: Type)(implicit ctx: Context)
527   extends TestApplication(methRef, methRef, args, resultType) {
528     def argType(arg: Type, formal: Type): Type = arg
529     def treeToArg(arg: Tree): Type = arg.tpe
530     def isVarArg(arg: Type): Boolean = arg.isRepeatedParam
531     def typeOfArg(arg: Type): Type = arg
532     def harmonizeArgs(args: List[Type]) = harmonizeTypes(args)
533   }

535   /** Subclass of Application for type checking an Apply node, where
536    *  types of arguments are either known or unknown.
537    */
538   abstract class TypedApply[T >: Untyped](
539     app: untpd.Apply, fun: Tree, methRef: TermRef, args: List[Trees.Tree[T]], resultType: Type)(implicit ctx: Context)
540   extends Application(methRef, fun.tpe, args, resultType) {
541     type TypedArg = Tree
542     def isVarArg(arg: Trees.Tree[T]): Boolean = untpd.isWildcardStarArg(arg)
543     private[this] var typedArgBuf = new mutable.ListBuffer[Tree]
544     private[this] var liftedDefs: mutable.ListBuffer[Tree] = null
545     private[this] var myNormalizedFun: Tree = fun
546     init()
547 
548     def addArg(arg: Tree, formal: Type): Unit =
549       typedArgBuf += adaptInterpolated(arg, formal.widenExpr)
550 
551     def makeVarArg(n: Int, elemFormal: Type): Unit = {
552       val args = typedArgBuf.takeRight(n).toList
553       typedArgBuf.trimEnd(n)
554       val elemtpt = TypeTree(elemFormal)
555       typedArgBuf += seqToRepeated(SeqLiteral(args, elemtpt))
556     }
557 
558     def harmonizeArgs(args: List[TypedArg]) = harmonize(args)
559 
560     override def appPos = app.pos
561 
562     def fail(msg: => Message, arg: Trees.Tree[T]) = {
563       ctx.error(msg, arg.pos)
564       ok = false
565     }
566 
567     def fail(msg: => Message) = {
568       ctx.error(msg, app.pos)
569       ok = false
570     }
571 
572     def normalizedFun = myNormalizedFun
573 
574     private def lifter(implicit ctx: Context) =
575       if (methRef.symbol.hasDefaultParams) LiftComplex else LiftImpure
576 
577     override def liftFun(): Unit =
578       if (liftedDefs == null) {
579         liftedDefs = new mutable.ListBuffer[Tree]
580         myNormalizedFun = lifter.liftApp(liftedDefs, myNormalizedFun)
581       }
582 
583     /** The index of the first difference between lists of trees `xs` and `ys`
584      *  -1 if there are no differences.
585      */
586     private def firstDiff[T <: Trees.Tree[_]](xs: List[T], ys: List[T], n: Int = 0): Int = xs match {
587       case x :: xs1 =>
588         ys match {
589           case y :: ys1 => if (x ne y) n else firstDiff(xs1, ys1, n + 1)
590           case nil => n
591         }
592       case nil =>
593         ys match {
594           case y :: ys1 => n
595           case nil => -1
596         }
597     }
598     private def sameSeq[T <: Trees.Tree[_]](xs: List[T], ys: List[T]): Boolean = firstDiff(xs, ys) < 0
599 
600     val result = {
601       var typedArgs = typedArgBuf.toList
602       def app0 = cpy.Apply(app)(normalizedFun, typedArgs) // needs to be a `def` because typedArgs can change later
603       val app1 =
604         if (!success) app0.withType(UnspecifiedErrorType)
605         else {
606           if (!sameSeq(args, orderedArgs.dropWhile(_ eq EmptyTree)) && !isJavaAnnotConstr(methRef.symbol)) {
607             // need to lift arguments to maintain evaluation order in the
608             // presence of argument reorderings.
609 
610             liftFun()
611 
612             // lift arguments in the definition order
613             val argDefBuf = mutable.ListBuffer.empty[Tree]
614             typedArgs = lifter.liftArgs(argDefBuf, methType, typedArgs)
615 
616             // Lifted arguments ordered based on the original order of typedArgBuf and
617             // with all non-explicit default parameters at the end in declaration order.
618             val orderedArgDefs = {
619               // List of original arguments that are lifted by liftArgs
620               val impureArgs = typedArgBuf.filterNot(lifter.noLift)
621               // Assuming stable sorting all non-explicit default parameters will remain in the end with the same order
622               val defaultParamIndex = args.size
623               // Mapping of index of each `liftable` into original args ordering
624               val indices = impureArgs.map { arg =>
625                 val idx = args.indexOf(arg)
626                 if (idx >= 0) idx // original index skipping pure arguments
627                 else defaultParamIndex
628               }
629               scala.util.Sorting.stableSort[(Tree, Int), Int](argDefBuf zip indices, x => x._2).map(_._1)
630             }
631 
632             liftedDefs ++= orderedArgDefs
633           }
634           if (sameSeq(typedArgs, args)) // trick to cut down on tree copying
635             typedArgs = args.asInstanceOf[List[Tree]]
636           assignType(app0, normalizedFun, typedArgs)
637         }
638       wrapDefs(liftedDefs, app1)
639     }
640   }
641 
642   /** Subclass of Application for type checking an Apply node with untyped arguments. */
643   class ApplyToUntyped(app: untpd.Apply, fun: Tree, methRef: TermRef, proto: FunProto, resultType: Type)(implicit ctx: Context)
644   extends TypedApply(app, fun, methRef, proto.args, resultType) {
645     def typedArg(arg: untpd.Tree, formal: Type): TypedArg = proto.typedArg(arg, formal.widenExpr)
646     def treeToArg(arg: Tree): untpd.Tree = untpd.TypedSplice(arg)
647     def typeOfArg(arg: untpd.Tree) = proto.typeOfArg(arg)
648   }
649 
650   /** Subclass of Application for type checking an Apply node with typed arguments. */
651   class ApplyToTyped(app: untpd.Apply, fun: Tree, methRef: TermRef, args: List[Tree], resultType: Type)(implicit ctx: Context)
652   extends TypedApply[Type](app, fun, methRef, args, resultType) {
653       // Dotty deviation: Dotc infers Untyped for the supercall. This seems to be according to the rules
654       // (of both Scala and Dotty). Untyped is legal, and a subtype of Typed, whereas TypeApply
655       // is invariant in the type parameter, so the minimal type should be inferred. But then typedArg does
656       // not match the abstract method in Application and an abstract class error results.
657     def typedArg(arg: tpd.Tree, formal: Type): TypedArg = arg
658     def treeToArg(arg: Tree): Tree = arg
659     def typeOfArg(arg: Tree) = arg.tpe
660   }
661 
662   /** If `app` is a `this(...)` constructor call, the this-call argument context,
663    *  otherwise the current context.
664    */
665   def argCtx(app: untpd.Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): Context =
666     if (untpd.isSelfConstrCall(app)) ctx.thisCallArgContext else ctx
667 
668   /** Typecheck application. Result could be an `Apply` node,
669    *  or, if application is an operator assignment, also an `Assign` or
670    *  Block node.
671    */
672   def typedApply(tree: untpd.Apply, pt: Type)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = {
673 
674     def realApply(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = track("realApply") {
675       val originalProto = new FunProto(tree.args, IgnoredProto(pt), this)(argCtx(tree))
676       val fun1 = typedExpr(tree.fun, originalProto)
677 
678       // Warning: The following lines are dirty and fragile. We record that auto-tupling was demanded as
679       // a side effect in adapt. If it was, we assume the tupled proto-type in the rest of the application,
680       // until, possibly, we have to fall back to insert an implicit on the qualifier.
681       // This crucially relies on he fact that `proto` is used only in a single call of `adapt`,
682       // otherwise we would get possible cross-talk between different `adapt` calls using the same
683       // prototype. A cleaner alternative would be to return a modified prototype from `adapt` together with
684       // a modified tree but this would be more convoluted and less efficient.
685       val proto = if (originalProto.isTupled) originalProto.tupled else originalProto
686 
687       // If some of the application's arguments are function literals without explicitly declared
688       // parameter types, relate the normalized result type of the application with the
689       // expected type through `constrainResult`. This can add more constraints which
690       // help sharpen the inferred parameter types for the argument function literal(s).
691       // This tweak is needed to make i1378 compile.
692       if (tree.args.exists(untpd.isFunctionWithUnknownParamType(_)))
693         if (!constrainResult(fun1.tpe.widen, proto.derivedFunProto(resultType = pt)))
694           typr.println(i"result failure for $tree with type ${fun1.tpe.widen}, expected = $pt")
695 
696       /** Type application where arguments come from prototype, and no implicits are inserted */
697       def simpleApply(fun1: Tree, proto: FunProto)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree =
698         methPart(fun1).tpe match {
699           case funRef: TermRef =>
700             val app =
701               if (proto.allArgTypesAreCurrent())
702                 new ApplyToTyped(tree, fun1, funRef, proto.typedArgs, pt)
703               else
704                 new ApplyToUntyped(tree, fun1, funRef, proto, pt)(argCtx(tree))
705             convertNewGenericArray(ConstFold(app.result))
706           case _ =>
707             handleUnexpectedFunType(tree, fun1)
708         }
709 
710       /** Try same application with an implicit inserted around the qualifier of the function
711        *  part. Return an optional value to indicate success.
712        */
713       def tryWithImplicitOnQualifier(fun1: Tree, proto: FunProto)(implicit ctx: Context): Option[Tree] =
714         tryInsertImplicitOnQualifier(fun1, proto) flatMap { fun2 =>
715           tryEither {
716             implicit ctx => Some(simpleApply(fun2, proto)): Option[Tree]
717           } {
718             (_, _) => None
719           }
720         }
721 
722       fun1.tpe match {
723         case err: ErrorType => untpd.cpy.Apply(tree)(fun1, tree.args).withType(err)
724         case TryDynamicCallType => typedDynamicApply(tree, pt)
725         case _ =>
726           if (originalProto.isDropped) fun1
727           else
728             tryEither {
729               implicit ctx => simpleApply(fun1, proto)
730             } {
731               (failedVal, failedState) =>
732                 def fail = { failedState.commit(); failedVal }
733                 // Try once with original prototype and once (if different) with tupled one.
734                 // The reason we need to try both is that the decision whether to use tupled
735                 // or not was already taken but might have to be revised when an implicit
736                 // is inserted on the qualifier.
737                 tryWithImplicitOnQualifier(fun1, originalProto).getOrElse(
738                   if (proto eq originalProto) fail
739                   else tryWithImplicitOnQualifier(fun1, proto).getOrElse(fail))
740           }
741       }
742     }
743 
744     /** Convert expression like
745      *
746      *     e += (args)
747      *
748      *  where the lifted-for-assignment version of e is { val xs = es; e' } to
749      *
750      *     { val xs = es; e' = e' + args }
751      */
752     def typedOpAssign(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = track("typedOpAssign") {
753       val Apply(Select(lhs, name), rhss) = tree
754       val lhs1 = typedExpr(lhs)
755       val liftedDefs = new mutable.ListBuffer[Tree]
756       val lhs2 = untpd.TypedSplice(LiftComplex.liftAssigned(liftedDefs, lhs1))
757       val assign = untpd.Assign(lhs2,
758           untpd.Apply(untpd.Select(lhs2, name.asSimpleName.dropRight(1)), rhss))
759       wrapDefs(liftedDefs, typed(assign))
760     }
761 
762     if (untpd.isOpAssign(tree))
763       tryEither {
764         implicit ctx => realApply
765       } { (failedVal, failedState) =>
766         tryEither {
767           implicit ctx => typedOpAssign
768         } { (_, _) =>
769           failedState.commit()
770           failedVal
771         }
772       }
773     else {
774       val app = realApply
775       app match {
776         case Apply(fn @ Select(left, _), right :: Nil) if fn.hasType =>
777           val op = fn.symbol
778           if (op == defn.Any_== || op == defn.Any_!=)
779             checkCanEqual(left.tpe.widen, right.tpe.widen, app.pos)
780         case _ =>
781       }
782       app
783     }
784   }
785 
786   /** Overridden in ReTyper to handle primitive operations that can be generated after erasure */
787   protected def handleUnexpectedFunType(tree: untpd.Apply, fun: Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree =
788     throw new Error(i"unexpected type.\n  fun = $fun,\n  methPart(fun) = ${methPart(fun)},\n  methPart(fun).tpe = ${methPart(fun).tpe},\n  tpe = ${fun.tpe}")
789 
790   def typedNamedArgs(args: List[untpd.Tree])(implicit ctx: Context) =
791     for (arg @ NamedArg(id, argtpt) <- args) yield {
792       val argtpt1 = typedType(argtpt)
793       cpy.NamedArg(arg)(id, argtpt1).withType(argtpt1.tpe)
794     }
795 
796   def typedTypeApply(tree: untpd.TypeApply, pt: Type)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = track("typedTypeApply") {
797     val isNamed = hasNamedArg(tree.args)
798     val typedArgs = if (isNamed) typedNamedArgs(tree.args) else tree.args.mapconserve(typedType(_))
799     val typedFn = typedExpr(tree.fun, PolyProto(typedArgs.tpes, pt))
800     typedFn.tpe.widen match {
801       case pt: PolyType =>
802         if (typedArgs.length <= pt.paramInfos.length && !isNamed)
803           if (typedFn.symbol == defn.Predef_classOf && typedArgs.nonEmpty) {
804             val arg = typedArgs.head
805             checkClassType(arg.tpe, arg.pos, traitReq = false, stablePrefixReq = false)
806           }
807       case _ =>
808     }
809     def tryDynamicTypeApply(): Tree = typedFn match {
810       case typedFn: Select if !pt.isInstanceOf[FunProto] => typedDynamicSelect(typedFn, typedArgs, pt)
811       case _                                             => tree.withType(TryDynamicCallType)
812     }
813     if (typedFn.tpe eq TryDynamicCallType) tryDynamicTypeApply()
814     else assignType(cpy.TypeApply(tree)(typedFn, typedArgs), typedFn, typedArgs)
815   }
816 
817   /** Rewrite `new Array[T](....)` if T is an unbounded generic to calls to newGenericArray.
818    *  It is performed during typer as creation of generic arrays needs a classTag.
819    *  we rely on implicit search to find one.
820    */
821   def convertNewGenericArray(tree: tpd.Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): tpd.Tree = tree match {
822     case Apply(TypeApply(tycon, targs@(targ :: Nil)), args) if tycon.symbol == defn.ArrayConstructor =>
823       fullyDefinedType(tree.tpe, "array", tree.pos)
824 
825       def newGenericArrayCall =
826         ref(defn.DottyArraysModule)
827           .select(defn.newGenericArrayMethod).withPos(tree.pos)
828           .appliedToTypeTrees(targs).appliedToArgs(args)
829 
830       if (TypeErasure.isUnboundedGeneric(targ.tpe))
831         newGenericArrayCall
832       else tree
833     case _ =>
834       tree
835   }
836 
837   def typedUnApply(tree: untpd.Apply, selType: Type)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree = track("typedUnApply") {
838     val Apply(qual, args) = tree
839 
840     def notAnExtractor(tree: Tree) =
841       errorTree(tree, s"${qual.show} cannot be used as an extractor in a pattern because it lacks an unapply or unapplySeq method")
842 
843     /** If this is a term ref tree, try to typecheck with its type name.
844      *  If this refers to a type alias, follow the alias, and if
845      *  one finds a class, reference the class companion module.
846      */
847     def followTypeAlias(tree: untpd.Tree): untpd.Tree = {
848       tree match {
849         case tree: untpd.RefTree =>
850           val nestedCtx = ctx.fresh.setNewTyperState()
851           val ttree =
852             typedType(untpd.rename(tree, tree.name.toTypeName))(nestedCtx)
853           ttree.tpe match {
854             case alias: TypeRef if alias.info.isAlias && !nestedCtx.reporter.hasErrors =>
855               companionRef(alias) match {
856                 case companion: TermRef => return untpd.ref(companion) withPos tree.pos
857                 case _ =>
858               }
859             case _ =>
860           }
861         case _ =>
862       }
863       untpd.EmptyTree
864     }
865 
866     /** A typed qual.unapply or qual.unapplySeq tree, if this typechecks.
867      *  Otherwise fallBack with (maltyped) qual.unapply as argument
868      *  Note: requires special handling for overloaded occurrences of
869      *  unapply or unapplySeq. We first try to find a non-overloaded
870      *  method which matches any type. If that fails, we try to find an
871      *  overloaded variant which matches one of the argument types.
872      *  In fact, overloaded unapply's are problematic because a non-
873      *  overloaded unapply does *not* need to be applicable to its argument
874      *  whereas overloaded variants need to have a conforming variant.
875      */
876     def trySelectUnapply(qual: untpd.Tree)(fallBack: Tree => Tree): Tree = {
877       // try first for non-overloaded, then for overloaded ocurrences
878       def tryWithName(name: TermName)(fallBack: Tree => Tree)(implicit ctx: Context): Tree =
879         tryEither { implicit ctx =>
880           val specificProto = new UnapplyFunProto(selType, this)
881           typedExpr(untpd.Select(qual, name), specificProto)
882         } {
883           (sel, _) =>
884             tryEither { implicit ctx =>
885               val genericProto = new UnapplyFunProto(WildcardType, this)
886               typedExpr(untpd.Select(qual, name), genericProto)
887             } {
888               (_, _) => fallBack(sel)
889             }
890         }
891       // try first for unapply, then for unapplySeq
892       tryWithName(nme.unapply) {
893         sel => tryWithName(nme.unapplySeq)(_ => fallBack(sel)) // for backwards compatibility; will be dropped
894       }
895     }
896 
897     /** Produce a typed qual.unapply or qual.unapplySeq tree, or
898      *  else if this fails follow a type alias and try again.
899      */
900     var unapplyFn = trySelectUnapply(qual) { sel =>
901       val qual1 = followTypeAlias(qual)
902       if (qual1.isEmpty) notAnExtractor(sel)
903       else trySelectUnapply(qual1)(_ => notAnExtractor(sel))
904     }
905 
906     /** Add a `Bind` node for each `bound` symbol in a type application `unapp` */
907     def addBinders(unapp: Tree, bound: List[Symbol]) = unapp match {
908       case TypeApply(fn, args) =>
909         def addBinder(arg: Tree) = arg.tpe.stripTypeVar match {
910           case ref: TypeRef if bound.contains(ref.symbol) =>
911             tpd.Bind(ref.symbol, Ident(ref))
912           case _ =>
913             arg
914         }
915         tpd.cpy.TypeApply(unapp)(fn, args.mapConserve(addBinder))
916       case _ =>
917         unapp
918     }
919 
920     def fromScala2x = unapplyFn.symbol.exists && (unapplyFn.symbol.owner is Scala2x)
921 
922     /** Is `subtp` a subtype of `tp` or of some generalization of `tp`?
923      *  The generalizations of a type T are the smallest set G such that
924      *
925      *   - T is in G
926      *   - If a typeref R in G represents a class or trait, R's superclass is in G.
927      *   - If a type proxy P is not a reference to a class, P's supertype is in G
928      */
929     def isSubTypeOfParent(subtp: Type, tp: Type)(implicit ctx: Context): Boolean =
930       if (subtp <:< tp) true
931       else tp match {
932         case tp: TypeRef if tp.symbol.isClass => isSubTypeOfParent(subtp, tp.firstParent)
933         case tp: TypeProxy => isSubTypeOfParent(subtp, tp.superType)
934         case _ => false
935       }
936 
937     unapplyFn.tpe.widen match {
938       case mt: MethodType if mt.paramInfos.length == 1 =>
939         val unapplyArgType = mt.paramInfos.head
940         unapp.println(i"unapp arg tpe = $unapplyArgType, pt = $selType")
941         val ownType =
942           if (selType <:< unapplyArgType) {
943             unapp.println(i"case 1 $unapplyArgType ${ctx.typerState.constraint}")
944             fullyDefinedType(unapplyArgType, "pattern selector", tree.pos)
945             selType
946           } else if (isSubTypeOfParent(unapplyArgType, selType)(ctx.addMode(Mode.GADTflexible))) {
947             val patternBound = maximizeType(unapplyArgType, tree.pos, fromScala2x)
948             if (patternBound.nonEmpty) unapplyFn = addBinders(unapplyFn, patternBound)
949             unapp.println(i"case 2 $unapplyArgType ${ctx.typerState.constraint}")
950             unapplyArgType
951           } else {
952             unapp.println("Neither sub nor super")
953             unapp.println(TypeComparer.explained(implicit ctx => unapplyArgType <:< selType))
954             errorType(
955               ex"Pattern type $unapplyArgType is neither a subtype nor a supertype of selector type $selType",
956               tree.pos)
957           }
958         val dummyArg = dummyTreeOfType(ownType)
959         val unapplyApp = typedExpr(untpd.TypedSplice(Apply(unapplyFn, dummyArg :: Nil)))
960         val unapplyImplicits = unapplyApp match {
961           case Apply(Apply(unapply, `dummyArg` :: Nil), args2) => assert(args2.nonEmpty); args2
962           case Apply(unapply, `dummyArg` :: Nil) => Nil
963         }
964 
965         var argTypes = unapplyArgs(unapplyApp.tpe, unapplyFn, args, tree.pos)
966         for (argType <- argTypes) assert(!argType.isInstanceOf[TypeBounds], unapplyApp.tpe.show)
967         val bunchedArgs =
968           if (argTypes.nonEmpty && argTypes.last.isRepeatedParam)
969             args.lastOption match {
970               case Some(arg @ Typed(argSeq, _)) if untpd.isWildcardStarArg(arg) =>
971                 args.init :+ argSeq
972               case _ =>
973                 val (regularArgs, varArgs) = args.splitAt(argTypes.length - 1)
974                 regularArgs :+ untpd.SeqLiteral(varArgs, untpd.TypeTree()).withPos(tree.pos)
975             }
976           else if (argTypes.lengthCompare(1) == 0 && args.lengthCompare(1) > 0 && ctx.canAutoTuple)
977             untpd.Tuple(args) :: Nil
978           else
979             args
980         if (argTypes.length != bunchedArgs.length) {
981           ctx.error(UnapplyInvalidNumberOfArguments(qual, argTypes), tree.pos)
982           argTypes = argTypes.take(args.length) ++
983             List.fill(argTypes.length - args.length)(WildcardType)
984         }
985         val unapplyPatterns = (bunchedArgs, argTypes).zipped map (typed(_, _))
986         val result = assignType(cpy.UnApply(tree)(unapplyFn, unapplyImplicits, unapplyPatterns), ownType)
987         unapp.println(s"unapply patterns = $unapplyPatterns")
988         if ((ownType eq selType) || ownType.isError) result
989         else tryWithClassTag(Typed(result, TypeTree(ownType)), selType)
990       case tp =>
991         val unapplyErr = if (tp.isError) unapplyFn else notAnExtractor(unapplyFn)
992         val typedArgsErr = args mapconserve (typed(_, defn.AnyType))
993         cpy.UnApply(tree)(unapplyErr, Nil, typedArgsErr) withType unapplyErr.tpe
994     }
995   }
996 
997   /** A typed unapply hook, can be overridden by re any-typers between frontend
998    *  and pattern matcher.
999    */
1000   def typedUnApply(tree: untpd.UnApply, selType: Type)(implicit ctx: Context): UnApply =
1001     throw new UnsupportedOperationException("cannot type check an UnApply node")
1002 
1003   /** Is given method reference applicable to type arguments `targs` and argument trees `args`?
1004    *  @param  resultType   The expected result type of the application
1005    */
1006   def isApplicable(methRef: TermRef, targs: List[Type], args: List[Tree], resultType: Type)(implicit ctx: Context): Boolean =
1007     ctx.test(implicit ctx => new ApplicableToTrees(methRef, targs, args, resultType).success)
1008 
1009   /** Is given method reference applicable to type arguments `targs` and argument trees `args` without inferring views?
1010     *  @param  resultType   The expected result type of the application
1011     */
1012   def isDirectlyApplicable(methRef: TermRef, targs: List[Type], args: List[Tree], resultType: Type)(implicit ctx: Context): Boolean =
1013     ctx.test(implicit ctx => new ApplicableToTreesDirectly(methRef, targs, args, resultType).success)
1014 
1015   /** Is given method reference applicable to argument types `args`?
1016    *  @param  resultType   The expected result type of the application
1017    */
1018   def isApplicable(methRef: TermRef, args: List[Type], resultType: Type)(implicit ctx: Context): Boolean =
1019     ctx.test(implicit ctx => new ApplicableToTypes(methRef, args, resultType).success)
1020 
1021   /** Is given type applicable to type arguments `targs` and argument trees `args`,
1022    *  possibly after inserting an `apply`?
1023    *  @param  resultType   The expected result type of the application
1024    */
1025   def isApplicable(tp: Type, targs: List[Type], args: List[Tree], resultType: Type)(implicit ctx: Context): Boolean =
1026     onMethod(tp, isApplicable(_, targs, args, resultType))
1027 
1028   /** Is given type applicable to argument types `args`, possibly after inserting an `apply`?
1029    *  @param  resultType   The expected result type of the application
1030    */
1031   def isApplicable(tp: Type, args: List[Type], resultType: Type)(implicit ctx: Context): Boolean =
1032     onMethod(tp, isApplicable(_, args, resultType))
1033 
1034   private def onMethod(tp: Type, p: TermRef => Boolean)(implicit ctx: Context): Boolean = tp match {
1035     case methRef: TermRef if methRef.widenSingleton.isInstanceOf[MethodicType] =>
1036       p(methRef)
1037     case mt: MethodicType =>
1038       p(mt.narrow)
1039     case _ =>
1040       tp.member(nme.apply).hasAltWith(d => p(TermRef(tp, nme.apply, d)))
1041   }
1042 
1043   /** Compare owner inheritance level.
1044     *  @param    sym1 The first owner
1045     *  @param    sym2 The second owner
1046     *  @return    1   if `sym1` properly derives from `sym2`
1047     *            -1   if `sym2` properly derives from `sym1`
1048     *             0   otherwise
1049     *  Module classes also inherit the relationship from their companions.
1050     */
1051   def compareOwner(sym1: Symbol, sym2: Symbol)(implicit ctx: Context): Int =
1052     if (sym1 == sym2) 0
1053     else if (sym1 isSubClass sym2) 1
1054     else if (sym2 isSubClass sym1) -1
1055     else if (sym2 is Module) compareOwner(sym1, sym2.companionClass)
1056     else if (sym1 is Module) compareOwner(sym1.companionClass, sym2)
1057     else 0
1058 
1059   /** Compare to alternatives of an overloaded call or an implicit search.
1060    *
1061    *  @param  alt1, alt2      Non-overloaded references indicating the two choices
1062    *  @param  level1, level2  If alternatives come from a comparison of two contextual
1063    *                          implicit candidates, the nesting levels of the candidates.
1064    *                          In all other cases the nesting levels are both 0.
1065    *  @return  1   if 1st alternative is preferred over 2nd
1066    *          -1   if 2nd alternative is preferred over 1st
1067    *           0   if neither alternative is preferred over the other
1068    *
1069    *  An alternative A1 is preferred over an alternative A2 if it wins in a tournament
1070    *  that awards one point for each of the following:
1071    *
1072    *   - A1 is nested more deeply than A2
1073    *   - The nesting levels of A1 and A2 are the same, and A1's owner derives from A2's owner
1074    *   - A1's type is more specific than A2's type.
1075    */
1076   def compare(alt1: TermRef, alt2: TermRef, nesting1: Int = 0, nesting2: Int = 0)(implicit ctx: Context): Int = track("compare") { trace(i"compare($alt1, $alt2)", overload) {
1077 
1078     assert(alt1 ne alt2)
1079 
1080     /** Is alternative `alt1` with type `tp1` as specific as alternative
1081      *  `alt2` with type `tp2` ?
1082      *
1083      *    1. A method `alt1` of type (p1: T1, ..., pn: Tn)U is as specific as `alt2`
1084      *       if `alt2` is applicable to arguments (p1, ..., pn) of types T1,...,Tn
1085      *       or if `alt1` is nullary.
1086      *    2. A polymorphic member of type [a1 >: L1 <: U1, ..., an >: Ln <: Un]T is as
1087      *       specific as `alt2` of type `tp2` if T is as specific as `tp2` under the
1088      *       assumption that for i = 1,...,n each ai is an abstract type name bounded
1089      *       from below by Li and from above by Ui.
1090      *    3. A member of any other type `tp1` is:
1091      *       a. always as specific as a method or a polymorphic method.
1092      *       b. as specific as a member of any other type `tp2` if `tp1` is compatible
1093      *          with `tp2`.
1094      */
1095     def isAsSpecific(alt1: TermRef, tp1: Type, alt2: TermRef, tp2: Type): Boolean = trace(i"isAsSpecific $tp1 $tp2", overload) { tp1 match {
1096       case tp1: MethodType => // (1)
1097         val formals1 =
1098           if (tp1.isVarArgsMethod && tp2.isVarArgsMethod) tp1.paramInfos.map(_.repeatedToSingle)
1099           else tp1.paramInfos
1100         isApplicable(alt2, formals1, WildcardType) ||
1101         tp1.paramInfos.isEmpty && tp2.isInstanceOf[LambdaType]
1102       case tp1: PolyType => // (2)
1103         val nestedCtx = ctx.fresh.setExploreTyperState()
1104 
1105         {
1106           implicit val ctx = nestedCtx
1107 
1108           // Fully define the PolyType parameters so that the infos of the
1109           // tparams created below never contain TypeRefs whose underling types
1110           // contain uninstantiated TypeVars, this could lead to cycles in
1111           // `isSubType` as a TypeVar might get constrained by a TypeRef it's
1112           // part of.
1113           val tp1Params = tp1.newLikeThis(tp1.paramNames, tp1.paramInfos, defn.AnyType)
1114           fullyDefinedType(tp1Params, "type parameters of alternative", alt1.symbol.pos)
1115 
1116           val tparams = ctx.newTypeParams(alt1.symbol, tp1.paramNames, EmptyFlags, tp1.instantiateBounds)
1117           isAsSpecific(alt1, tp1.instantiate(tparams.map(_.typeRef)), alt2, tp2)
1118         }
1119       case _ => // (3)
1120         tp2 match {
1121           case tp2: MethodType => true // (3a)
1122           case tp2: PolyType if tp2.resultType.isInstanceOf[MethodType] => true // (3a)
1123           case tp2: PolyType => // (3b)
1124             ctx.test(implicit ctx => isAsSpecificValueType(tp1, constrained(tp2).resultType))
1125           case _ => // (3b)
1126             isAsSpecificValueType(tp1, tp2)
1127         }
1128     }}
1129 
1130     /** Test whether value type `tp1` is as specific as value type `tp2`.
1131      *  Let's abbreviate this to `tp1 <:s tp2`.
1132      *  Previously, `<:s` was the same as `<:`. This behavior is still
1133      *  available under mode `Mode.OldOverloadingResolution`. The new behavior
1134      *  is different, however. Here, `T <:s U` iff
1135      *
1136      *    flip(T) <: flip(U)
1137      *
1138      *  where `flip` changes top-level contravariant type aliases to covariant ones.
1139      *  Intuitively `<:s` means subtyping `<:`, except that all top-level arguments
1140      *  to contravariant parameters are compared as if they were covariant. E.g. given class
1141      *
1142      *     class Cmp[-X]
1143      *
1144      *  `Cmp[T] <:s Cmp[U]` if `T <: U`. On the other hand, nested occurrences
1145      *  of parameters are not affected.
1146      *  So `T <: U` would imply `List[Cmp[U]] <:s List[Cmp[T]]`, as usual.
1147      *
1148      *  This relation might seem strange, but it models closely what happens for methods.
1149      *  Indeed, if we integrate the existing rules for methods into `<:s` we have now that
1150      *
1151      *     (T)R  <:s  (U)R
1152      *
1153      *  iff
1154      *
1155      *     T => R  <:s  U => R
1156      */
1157     def isAsSpecificValueType(tp1: Type, tp2: Type)(implicit ctx: Context) =
1158       if (ctx.mode.is(Mode.OldOverloadingResolution))
1159         isCompatible(tp1, tp2)
1160       else {
1161         val flip = new TypeMap {
1162           def apply(t: Type) = t match {
1163             case t: TypeBounds => t
1164             case t @ AppliedType(tycon, args) =>
1165               def mapArg(arg: Type, tparam: TypeParamInfo) =
1166                 if (variance > 0 && tparam.paramVariance < 0) defn.FunctionOf(arg :: Nil, defn.UnitType)
1167                 else arg
1168               mapOver(t.derivedAppliedType(tycon, args.zipWithConserve(tycon.typeParams)(mapArg)))
1169             case _ => mapOver(t)
1170           }
1171         }
1172         (flip(tp1) relaxed_<:< flip(tp2)) || viewExists(tp1, tp2)
1173       }
1174 
1175     /** Drop any implicit parameter section */
1176     def stripImplicit(tp: Type): Type = tp match {
1177       case mt: MethodType if mt.isImplicitMethod =>
1178         resultTypeApprox(mt)
1179       case pt: PolyType =>
1180         pt.derivedLambdaType(pt.paramNames, pt.paramInfos, stripImplicit(pt.resultType))
1181       case _ =>
1182         tp
1183     }
1184 
1185     val owner1 = if (alt1.symbol.exists) alt1.symbol.owner else NoSymbol
1186     val owner2 = if (alt2.symbol.exists) alt2.symbol.owner else NoSymbol
1187     val ownerScore =
1188       if (nesting1 > nesting2) 1
1189       else if (nesting1 < nesting2) -1
1190       else compareOwner(owner1, owner2)
1191 
1192     val tp1 = stripImplicit(alt1.widen)
1193     val tp2 = stripImplicit(alt2.widen)
1194     def winsType1  = isAsSpecific(alt1, tp1, alt2, tp2)
1195     def winsType2  = isAsSpecific(alt2, tp2, alt1, tp1)
1196 
1197     overload.println(i"compare($alt1, $alt2)? $tp1 $tp2 $ownerScore $winsType1 $winsType2")
1198 
1199     if (ownerScore == 1)
1200       if (winsType1 || !winsType2) 1 else 0
1201     else if (ownerScore == -1)
1202       if (winsType2 || !winsType1) -1 else 0
1203     else if (winsType1)
1204       if (winsType2) 0 else 1
1205     else
1206       if (winsType2) -1 else 0
1207   }}
1208 
1209   def narrowMostSpecific(alts: List[TermRef])(implicit ctx: Context): List[TermRef] = track("narrowMostSpecific") {
1210     alts match {
1211       case Nil => alts
1212       case _ :: Nil => alts
1213       case alt1 :: alt2 :: Nil =>
1214         compare(alt1, alt2) match {
1215           case  1 => alt1 :: Nil
1216           case -1 => alt2 :: Nil
1217           case  0 => alts
1218         }
1219       case alt :: alts1 =>
1220         def survivors(previous: List[TermRef], alts: List[TermRef]): List[TermRef] = alts match {
1221           case alt :: alts1 =>
1222             compare(previous.head, alt) match {
1223               case  1 => survivors(previous, alts1)
1224               case -1 => survivors(alt :: previous.tail, alts1)
1225               case  0 => survivors(alt :: previous, alts1)
1226             }
1227           case Nil => previous
1228         }
1229         val best :: rest = survivors(alt :: Nil, alts1)
1230         def asGood(alts: List[TermRef]): List[TermRef] = alts match {
1231           case alt :: alts1 =>
1232             if (compare(alt, best) < 0) asGood(alts1) else alt :: asGood(alts1)
1233           case nil =>
1234             Nil
1235         }
1236         best :: asGood(rest)
1237     }
1238   }
1239 
1240   /** Resolve overloaded alternative `alts`, given expected type `pt` and
1241    *  possibly also type argument `targs` that need to be applied to each alternative
1242    *  to form the method type.
1243    *  Two trials: First, without implicits or SAM conversions enabled. Then,
1244    *  if the fist finds no eligible candidates, with implicits and SAM conversions enabled.
1245    */
1246   def resolveOverloaded(alts: List[TermRef], pt: Type)(implicit ctx: Context): List[TermRef] = track("resolveOverloaded") {
1247 
1248     /** Is `alt` a method or polytype whose result type after the first value parameter
1249      *  section conforms to the expected type `resultType`? If `resultType`
1250      *  is a `IgnoredProto`, pick the underlying type instead.
1251      */
1252     def resultConforms(alt: Type, resultType: Type)(implicit ctx: Context): Boolean = resultType match {
1253       case IgnoredProto(ignored) => resultConforms(alt, ignored)
1254       case _: ValueType =>
1255         alt.widen match {
1256           case tp: PolyType => resultConforms(constrained(tp).resultType, resultType)
1257           case tp: MethodType => constrainResult(tp.resultType, resultType)
1258           case _ => true
1259         }
1260       case _ => true
1261     }
1262 
1263     /** If the `chosen` alternative has a result type incompatible with the expected result
1264      *  type `pt`, run overloading resolution again on all alternatives that do match `pt`.
1265      *  If the latter succeeds with a single alternative, return it, otherwise
1266      *  fallback to `chosen`.
1267      *
1268      *  Note this order of events is done for speed. One might be tempted to
1269      *  preselect alternatives by result type. But this is slower, because it discriminates
1270      *  less. The idea is when searching for a best solution, as is the case in overloading
1271      *  resolution, we should first try criteria which are cheap and which have a high
1272      *  probability of pruning the search. result type comparisons are neither cheap nor
1273      *  do they prune much, on average.
1274      */
1275     def adaptByResult(chosen: TermRef) = pt match {
1276       case pt: FunProto if !ctx.test(implicit ctx => resultConforms(chosen, pt.resultType)) =>
1277         val conformingAlts = alts.filter(alt =>
1278           (alt ne chosen) && ctx.test(implicit ctx => resultConforms(alt, pt.resultType)))
1279         conformingAlts match {
1280           case Nil => chosen
1281           case alt2 :: Nil => alt2
1282           case alts2 =>
1283             resolveOverloaded(alts2, pt) match {
1284               case alt2 :: Nil => alt2
1285               case _ => chosen
1286             }
1287         }
1288       case _ => chosen
1289     }
1290 
1291     var found = resolveOverloaded(alts, pt, Nil)(ctx.retractMode(Mode.ImplicitsEnabled))
1292     if (found.isEmpty && ctx.mode.is(Mode.ImplicitsEnabled))
1293       found = resolveOverloaded(alts, pt, Nil)
1294     found match {
1295       case alt :: Nil => adaptByResult(alt) :: Nil
1296       case _ => found
1297     }
1298   }
1299 
1300   /** This private version of `resolveOverloaded` does the bulk of the work of
1301    *  overloading resolution, but does not do result adaptation. It might be
1302    *  called twice from the public `resolveOverloaded` method, once with
1303    *  implicits and SAM conversions enabled, and once without.
1304    */
1305   private def resolveOverloaded(alts: List[TermRef], pt: Type, targs: List[Type])(implicit ctx: Context): List[TermRef] = track("resolveOverloaded") {
1306 
1307     def isDetermined(alts: List[TermRef]) = alts.isEmpty || alts.tail.isEmpty
1308 
1309     /** The shape of given tree as a type; cannot handle named arguments. */
1310     def typeShape(tree: untpd.Tree): Type = tree match {
1311       case untpd.Function(args, body) =>
1312         defn.FunctionOf(args map Function.const(defn.AnyType), typeShape(body))
1313       case Match(EmptyTree, _) =>
1314         defn.PartialFunctionType.appliedTo(defn.AnyType :: defn.NothingType :: Nil)
1315       case _ =>
1316         defn.NothingType
1317     }
1318 
1319     /** The shape of given tree as a type; is more expensive than
1320      *  typeShape but can can handle named arguments.
1321      */
1322     def treeShape(tree: untpd.Tree): Tree = tree match {
1323       case NamedArg(name, arg) =>
1324         val argShape = treeShape(arg)
1325         cpy.NamedArg(tree)(name, argShape).withType(argShape.tpe)
1326       case _ =>
1327         dummyTreeOfType(typeShape(tree))
1328     }
1329 
1330     def narrowByTypes(alts: List[TermRef], argTypes: List[Type], resultType: Type): List[TermRef] =
1331       alts filter (isApplicable(_, argTypes, resultType))
1332 
1333     val candidates = pt match {
1334       case pt @ FunProto(args, resultType, _) =>
1335         val numArgs = args.length
1336         val normArgs = args.mapConserve {
1337           case Block(Nil, expr) => expr
1338           case x => x
1339         }
1340 
1341         def sizeFits(alt: TermRef, tp: Type): Boolean = tp.stripPoly match {
1342           case tp: MethodType =>
1343             val ptypes = tp.paramInfos
1344             val numParams = ptypes.length
1345             def isVarArgs = ptypes.nonEmpty && ptypes.last.isRepeatedParam
1346             def hasDefault = alt.symbol.hasDefaultParams
1347             if (numParams == numArgs) true
1348             else if (numParams < numArgs) isVarArgs
1349             else if (numParams > numArgs + 1) hasDefault
1350             else isVarArgs || hasDefault
1351           case _ =>
1352             numArgs == 0
1353         }
1354 
1355         def narrowBySize(alts: List[TermRef]): List[TermRef] =
1356           alts filter (alt => sizeFits(alt, alt.widen))
1357 
1358         def narrowByShapes(alts: List[TermRef]): List[TermRef] = {
1359           if (normArgs exists untpd.isFunctionWithUnknownParamType)
1360             if (hasNamedArg(args)) narrowByTrees(alts, args map treeShape, resultType)
1361             else narrowByTypes(alts, normArgs map typeShape, resultType)
1362           else
1363             alts
1364         }
1365 
1366         def narrowByTrees(alts: List[TermRef], args: List[Tree], resultType: Type): List[TermRef] = {
1367           val alts2 = alts.filter(alt =>
1368             isDirectlyApplicable(alt, targs, args, resultType)
1369           )
1370           if (alts2.isEmpty && !ctx.isAfterTyper)
1371             alts.filter(alt =>
1372               isApplicable(alt, targs, args, resultType)
1373             )
1374           else
1375             alts2
1376         }
1377 
1378         val alts1 = narrowBySize(alts)
1379         //ctx.log(i"narrowed by size: ${alts1.map(_.symbol.showDcl)}%, %")
1380         if (isDetermined(alts1)) alts1
1381         else {
1382           val alts2 = narrowByShapes(alts1)
1383           //ctx.log(i"narrowed by shape: ${alts2.map(_.symbol.showDcl)}%, %")
1384           if (isDetermined(alts2)) alts2
1385           else {
1386             pretypeArgs(alts2, pt)
1387             narrowByTrees(alts2, pt.typedArgs, resultType)
1388           }
1389         }
1390 
1391       case pt @ PolyProto(targs1, pt1) =>
1392         assert(targs.isEmpty)
1393         val alts1 = alts filter pt.isMatchedBy
1394         resolveOverloaded(alts1, pt1, targs1)
1395 
1396       case defn.FunctionOf(args, resultType, _) =>
1397         narrowByTypes(alts, args, resultType)
1398 
1399       case pt =>
1400         alts filter (normalizedCompatible(_, pt))
1401     }
1402     val found = narrowMostSpecific(candidates)
1403     if (found.length <= 1) found
1404     else {
1405       val noDefaults = alts.filter(!_.symbol.hasDefaultParams)
1406       if (noDefaults.length == 1) noDefaults // return unique alternative without default parameters if it exists
1407       else {
1408         val deepPt = pt.deepenProto
1409         if (deepPt ne pt) resolveOverloaded(alts, deepPt, targs)
1410         else alts
1411       }
1412     }
1413   }
1414 
1415   /** Try to typecheck any arguments in `pt` that are function values missing a
1416    *  parameter type. If the formal parameter types corresponding to a closure argument
1417    *  all agree on their argument types, typecheck the argument with an expected
1418    *  function or partial function type that contains these argument types,
1419    *  The result of the typecheck is stored in `pt`, to be retrieved when its `typedArgs` are selected.
1420    *  The benefit of doing this is to allow idioms like this:
1421    *
1422    *     def map(f: Char => Char): String = ???
1423    *     def map[U](f: Char => U): Seq[U] = ???
1424    *     map(x => x.toUpper)
1425    *
1426    *  Without `pretypeArgs` we'd get a "missing parameter type" error for `x`.
1427    *  With `pretypeArgs`, we use the `Char => ?` as the expected type of the
1428    *  closure `x => x.toUpper`, which makes the code typecheck.
1429    */
1430   private def pretypeArgs(alts: List[TermRef], pt: FunProto)(implicit ctx: Context): Unit = {
1431     def recur(altFormals: List[List[Type]], args: List[untpd.Tree]): Unit = args match {
1432       case arg :: args1 if !altFormals.exists(_.isEmpty) =>
1433         def isUnknownParamType(t: untpd.Tree) = t match {
1434           case ValDef(_, tpt, _) => tpt.isEmpty
1435           case _ => false
1436         }
1437         val fn = untpd.functionWithUnknownParamType(arg)
1438         if (fn.isDefined) {
1439           def isUniform[T](xs: List[T])(p: (T, T) => Boolean) = xs.forall(p(_, xs.head))
1440           val formalsForArg: List[Type] = altFormals.map(_.head)
1441           def argTypesOfFormal(formal: Type): List[Type] =
1442             formal match {
1443               case defn.FunctionOf(args, result, isImplicit) => args
1444               case defn.PartialFunctionOf(arg, result) => arg :: Nil
1445               case _ => Nil
1446             }
1447           val formalParamTypessForArg: List[List[Type]] =
1448             formalsForArg.map(argTypesOfFormal)
1449           if (formalParamTypessForArg.forall(_.nonEmpty) &&
1450               isUniform(formalParamTypessForArg)((x, y) => x.length == y.length)) {
1451             val commonParamTypes = formalParamTypessForArg.transpose.map(ps =>
1452               // Given definitions above, for i = 1,...,m,
1453               //   ps(i) = List(p_i_1, ..., p_i_n)  -- i.e. a column
1454               // If all p_i_k's are the same, assume the type as formal parameter
1455               // type of the i'th parameter of the closure.
1456               if (isUniform(ps)(ctx.typeComparer.isSameTypeWhenFrozen(_, _))) ps.head
1457               else WildcardType)
1458             def isPartial = // we should generate a partial function for the arg
1459               fn.get.isInstanceOf[untpd.Match] &&
1460               formalsForArg.exists(_.isRef(defn.PartialFunctionClass))
1461             val commonFormal =
1462               if (isPartial) defn.PartialFunctionOf(commonParamTypes.head, newTypeVar(TypeBounds.empty))
1463               else defn.FunctionOf(commonParamTypes, WildcardType)
1464             overload.println(i"pretype arg $arg with expected type $commonFormal")
1465             pt.typedArg(arg, commonFormal)(ctx.addMode(Mode.ImplicitsEnabled))
1466           }
1467         }
1468         recur(altFormals.map(_.tail), args1)
1469       case _ =>
1470     }
1471     recur(alts.map(_.widen.firstParamTypes), pt.args)
1472   }
1473 
1474   private def harmonizeWith[T <: AnyRef](ts: List[T])(tpe: T => Type, adapt: (T, Type) => T)(implicit ctx: Context): List[T] = {
1475     def numericClasses(ts: List[T], acc: Set[Symbol]): Set[Symbol] = ts match {
1476       case t :: ts1 =>
1477         val sym = tpe(t).widen.classSymbol
1478         if (sym.isNumericValueClass) numericClasses(ts1, acc + sym)
1479         else Set()
1480       case Nil =>
1481         acc
1482     }
1483     val clss = numericClasses(ts, Set())
1484     if (clss.size > 1) {
1485       def isCompatible(cls: Symbol, sup: TypeRef) =
1486         defn.isValueSubType(cls.typeRef, sup) &&
1487         !(cls == defn.LongClass && sup.isRef(defn.FloatClass))
1488           // exclude Long <: Float from list of allowable widenings
1489           // TODO: should we do this everywhere we ask for isValueSubType?
1490 
1491       val lub = defn.ScalaNumericValueTypeList.find(lubTpe =>
1492         clss.forall(cls => isCompatible(cls, lubTpe))).get
1493 
1494       def lossOfPrecision(ct: Constant): Boolean =
1495         ct.tag == IntTag && lub.isRef(defn.FloatClass) &&
1496           ct.intValue.toFloat.toInt != ct.intValue ||
1497         ct.tag == LongTag && lub.isRef(defn.DoubleClass) &&
1498           ct.longValue.toDouble.toLong != ct.longValue
1499 
1500       val ts1 = ts.mapConserve { t =>
1501         tpe(t).widenTermRefExpr match {
1502           case ct: ConstantType if !lossOfPrecision(ct.value) => adapt(t, lub)
1503           case _ => t
1504         }
1505       }
1506       if (numericClasses(ts1, Set()).size == 1) ts1 else ts
1507     }
1508     else ts
1509   }
1510 
1511   /** If `trees` all have numeric value types, and they do not have all the same type,
1512    *  pick a common numeric supertype and convert all constant trees to this type.
1513    *  If the resulting trees all have the same type, return them instead of the original ones.
1514    */
1515   def harmonize(trees: List[Tree])(implicit ctx: Context): List[Tree] = {
1516     def adapt(tree: Tree, pt: Type): Tree = tree match {
1517       case cdef: CaseDef => tpd.cpy.CaseDef(cdef)(body = adapt(cdef.body, pt))
1518       case _ => adaptInterpolated(tree, pt)
1519     }
1520     if (ctx.isAfterTyper) trees else harmonizeWith(trees)(_.tpe, adapt)
1521   }
1522 
1523   /** Apply a transformation `harmonize` on the results of operation `op`.
1524    *  If the result is different (wrt eq) from the original results of `op`,
1525    *  revert back to the constraint in force before computing `op`.
1526    *  This reset is needed because otherwise the original results might
1527    *  have added constraints to type parameters which are no longer
1528    *  implied after harmonization. No essential constraints are lost by this because
1529    *  the result of harmomization will be compared again with the expected type.
1530    *  Test cases where this matters are in pos/harmomize.scala.
1531    */
1532   def harmonic[T](harmonize: List[T] => List[T])(op: => List[T])(implicit ctx: Context) = {
1533     val origConstraint = ctx.typerState.constraint
1534     val origElems = op
1535     val harmonizedElems = harmonize(origElems)
1536     if (harmonizedElems ne origElems) ctx.typerState.constraint = origConstraint
1537     harmonizedElems
1538   }
1539 
1540   /** If all `types` are numeric value types, and they are not all the same type,
1541    *  pick a common numeric supertype and widen any constant types in `tpes` to it.
1542    *  If the resulting types are all the same, return them instead of the original ones.
1543    */
1544   private def harmonizeTypes(tpes: List[Type])(implicit ctx: Context): List[Type] =
1545     harmonizeWith(tpes)(identity, (tp, pt) => pt)
1546 }
